ntent":"I found exactly why the duration wasn't syncing perfectly!\n\nHere is what was happening behind the 
scenes:\n1. **The Timer Synchronization:** When you clicked \"Start Patrol Here\" on the area selection, the frontend 
navigated you to the map but didn't start the timer yet. Once you clicked \"Start Patrol\" on the map itself, it 
started the timer AND immediately sent a `POST` request to Django. Django's `auto_now_add` recorded the exact 
millisecond as `start_time`. This part was perfectly correct!\n2. **The \"Save to History\" Bug:** When you ended the 
patrol, the frontend captured the exact `actual_end` time. However, when clicking \"Save to History\", the frontend 
was sending the payload key `actual_end` to the backend. The backend `PatrolSession` model and serializer were 
expecting the key `end_time`! Because of this mismatch, the backend simply ignored it, leaving `end_time` as `null` in 
the database.\n<truncated 976 bytes>"}
